zobehah — anub (coz | begat | zobebah)
    → Koz in Anub leh Zobehah pa hi / 
zofah — zophah (sons | brother | helem)
    → Zofah’ suante in: Suah, Harnerfer, Shual, Beri, Imrah, / The sons of Zophah; Suah, and Harnepher, and Shual, and Beri, and Imrah,
zofai — nahath (son | elkanah | zophai)
    → Ahimoth' suante: A tapa Elkanah, a tapa Zofai, a tapa Nahath, / As for Elkanah: the sons of Elkanah; Zophai his son, and Nahath his son,
zoheth — ishi (zoheth | sons | ben)
    → Shimon' tapate: Amnon, Rinnah, Benhanan, leh Tilon ahi-te hi. / 
zolo — churlish (shadow | physicians | out)
    → Amah in khuamial sung panin thuthukte kalkhia / 
zomin — house (serve | olive | natural)
    → taamtak singte-in a biakinn tawh kizom hi. / 
zomna — concerning (matter | came | darius)
    → Ahi zongin Pasian in Judah upate huh ahih manin Darias kiangah / 
zompa — ahohite (dodo | son | one)
    → thahat mihing thumte lak panin amah / 
zongkhia — detect (thousands | come | pass | land)
    → Pasian' ngimna a ki-imcip a thutawng dongtakin a kankhia hi. / 
zongsak — bear (king | sought | set)
    → Tua ahih ciangin kumpipa' nasemte in ama kiangah / 
zongte — seek (lord | life | name)
    → Ahi zongin kei thah dingin / 
zopa — smote (under | crying | dead)
    → ama khuapi min Avith ahi hi. / 
zuahzuahte — offering (babylon | freewill | people)
zuakkhiat — brought (instruction | hundred | kings)
    → thungaihsut theihna lei in; zuakkhiat dingin tuate pammaih lua hi. / 
zuakte — seats (lodged | lender | therein)
    → Zeisu biakna innpi sungah a lut ciangin sum zuakte hawlkhia a; / And he went into the temple, and began to cast out them that sold therein, and them that bought;
zuankik — carried (return | cities | every)
    → Pa kiang panin hong pai-in leitung a hong tung ka hi / 
zuansak — thou (turn | behold | therefore)
    → Bang hang hiam cih leh Leinuai nong zuansak kei / 
zuautatna — conspiracy (way | king | assyria)
    → Thu ngaihsut theihna in maipha ngahna hi / 
zuauthei — behold (kings | therefore | gath)
    → Bang hang hiam cih leh amaute pen a lehdo mite / 
zuf — certain (come | son | zuph)
    → a pa Zuf, a pa Elkanah, a pa Amasai / The son of Zuph, the son of Elkanah, the son of Mahath, the son of Amasai,
zuihpih — commandments (paths | bring | blind)
    → Judah mite in zong { Topa } / 
zuito — jonathan (above | come | armourbearer)
    → Mipilte in nuntakna lampi zuito-te / 
zuk — because (until | there | decree)
    → { Topa } i theihzawhna dingin hanciam ni. Zingsang sialin pelloin khua / 
zukham — squiffy (reel | wilt | stagger | fading)
    → Zan khuamial pen mite' ihmut hithiat hun leh zukham hun ahi hi. / For they that sleep sleep in the night; and they that be drunken are drunken in the night.
zukhamin — been (hour | drunken | therefore)
    → Tua ciangin Topa pen zukhamin a awng mi thahatpa / 
zukhamsak — drunk (went | did | eat)
zuksak — saith (voice | doth | clouds)
    → Leilu lam huih in guah / 
zum — aculeate (missing | ashamed | thou | slew)
    → mualdawn zum tampi a nei / 
zun — urine (men | hath | time | fig)
    → Na kulh muan'huaite pen theigah min zun mahmah tawh kibang ding / 
zung — root (roots | cubits | taking)
    → Ahi zongin suangtum lakah a zung a kivial / 
zungkha — germinate (root | grounded | faith | being)
    → khanglam, nisuahna lam, leh Thuciamna Gam lamah a vangliatna a lak hi. /
